<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проделать.html>проде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodélatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проделывать.html>проде́лывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodélyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проделать.html>проде́лать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make (a hole), to break through (a hole)</li>
<li>to do (a trick)</li>
<li>to carry out (a task; work)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продержаться.html>продержа́ться</a> (8644)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продержать.html>продержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продержаться.html>продержа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proderžátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to hold out, to stand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(food)</i> to keep <i>(fresh)</i>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продержать.html>продержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***продлевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продлевать.html>продлева́ть</a> (25106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продлить.html>продли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with irregular sound change.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продлевать.html>продлева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodlevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продлить.html>продли́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to extend, to prolong, to elongate, to make longer</li>
<li>to renew, to extend (e.g. subscriptions, books in a library)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>прод<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:продлить.html>продли́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>про-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-дл-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ева</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">длить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продлить.html>продли́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodlítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продлевать.html>продлева́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">продля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to extend, to prolong, to elongate, to make longer</li>
<li>to renew, to extend (e.g. subscriptions, books in a library)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продолжать.html>продолжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodolžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продолжить.html>продо́лжить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to continue, to proceed (with), to go on</li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дол.html>до́л</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></b>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дол-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dol-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Expected form based on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:длина.html>длина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dliná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> would be <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*проде́льный</span>; form with <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-о-</span> influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dólgij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***продрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продрать.html>продрать</a> (19039)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>дра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продрать.html>продра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">продира́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hole, to tear holes <i>(in)</i>, to wear out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:продрать.html>продра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prodrátʹ</b> glaza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to open one's eyes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>ко́гтем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продрать.html>продра́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:медведь.html>медве́дь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мешок.html>мешке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дырка.html>ды́рку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>поднял</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вытряхивать.html>вытря́хивать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>муку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голову</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:подхватывать.html>подхва́тывая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языко́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kógtem <b>prodrál</b> medvédʹ v mešké dýrku, podnjal jevó i stal vytrjáxivatʹ muku sebé na golovu, podxvátyvaja jejó jazykóm</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">with the claws, the bear <b>tore</b> a hole in the sack, lifted it and began shaking it atop the head collecting [the content] with the tongue</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
